first transgender to anchor a daily television news show and she has been
grabbing attention in the southern state of Tamil Nadu.</span></div></div></textarea>

</h2>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4868130380564566879' itemprop='description articleBody'>

 to someone with rancid breath or even worse if you end up in bed with 
someone who has become one with body odour.</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
Yes, my fellow Nigerians. Quite a number of you smell. Be it body or 
mouth odour but it has become a threat to social existence in our 
society because some of you are so selfish and too wicked to bother 
about personal hygiene. Only money money money una de think? It&#8217;s not 
fair ooooo.</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<span class="IL_AD" id="IL_AD8">Come on people</span>, do you know that the way you smell can even favour or be bad luck to you when you are trying to get employed?</div>

realities on the ground in Rivers.<br><br>President Jonathan had during a

</h2>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7386246592945781456' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<textarea id='postData-7386246592945781456' style='display:none;'><div style="text-align: center;">

path of caution by allowing God to judge his own case instead of 
dragging the body of Christ in the mud.</div>

<article class='post hentry' id='117860880043813466' itemscope='' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<h2 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name headline'>
<a href='http://www.ocbvibez.blogspot.com/2014/09/troops-boko-haram-resume-fight-in.html' itemprop='url'>Troops, Boko Haram Resume Fight in Konduga</a>
</h2>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-117860880043813466' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<textarea id='postData-117860880043813466' style='display:none;'><div style="text-align: center;">
<script async="" src="//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js"></script>

</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<ins class="adsbygoogle" data-ad-client="ca-pub-8102695603251980" data-ad-slot="5498490356" style="display: inline-block; height: 280px; width: 336px;"></ins></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<script>
(adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
</script></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-X8oIJ59sLb8/VCbTsQYLyBI/AAAAAAAAq48/dn_-OKbjkPI/s1600/Military.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-X8oIJ59sLb8/VCbTsQYLyBI/AAAAAAAAq48/dn_-OKbjkPI/s1600/Military.jpg"></a></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<br></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
The battle to return the north eastern region of Nigeria back to normalcy saw its hottest battle on Friday in Konduga. Information indicates that both the Nigerian military and the Jihadist group sustained heavy casualty in the battle to regain the town. Available information suggests the Jihadist group launched a night attack on Konduga town on Thursday, but they were surprised by a more patriotic Nigerian force than they were used to.  A heated battle between the Nigerian forces and the Jihadist group ensued &#8211; resulting in the loss of lives from both camps in significant numbers.</div>
</textarea>

<strong><a href='http://www.ocbvibez.blogspot.com/2014/09/troops-boko-haram-resume-fight-in.html' title='Troops, Boko Haram Resume Fight in Konduga'>Troops, Boko Haram Resume Fight in Konduga</a></strong>
<p>             The battle to return the north eastern region of Nigeria back to normalcy saw its hotte...</p>
</div>
